## Text Elements

1 + 2 + 3 + ... + 300 ^rd1WCEtY

First number: 1 ^soYBZMn4

Last number: 300 ^J9lL73H4

Each pair (like 1 + 300, 2 + 299, etc.) adds up to: ^Lmk3wECF

1 + 300 = 301 ^YCuND3iu

Number of such pairs: ^48z3poim

Since there are 300 numbers total, you get ^hb2TnLAq

300 ÷ 2 = 150 pairs ^5mzihjeU

n(A U B) = n(A) + n(B) - n(A∩B) ^5IOXHsV1
